Overview of Flood Conditions in Various Counties and Cities in Hubei 51

Hankou: After the breaches at Danshui Pool and Dandong Gate, the entire city of Hankou, except for the highest ground in Dajia Street and Huangpi Street, which retained a little dry land, was completely flooded. The deepest areas reached two zhang, and even the shallower areas were several feet deep. The deaths of people and livestock, as well as the loss of property, were countless. It is estimated that there are over 200,000 refugees in the entire town. (Relief measures) The Emergency Flood Relief Association sends people daily to distribute steamed buns per person.

Baisha Zhou and newly silted Zhou areas under the jurisdiction of Wuchang County are low-lying and have long become a watery realm. All houses and utensils have been submerged. After July 27th, the Wu Tai Ding Gong Temple long embankment and the Wu Qing Dike Gate were successively breached. The residents' fields and houses inside the embankment were completely swept away. The upper reaches of the provincial capital became a vast expanse of water. On the 28th, two breaches occurred in the Yongbao Embankment, and on the 29th, three breaches occurred in the Wuhui Embankment. Residents inside the embankment with lower foundations had no time to care for their houses and belongings. The Bajiyongfeng area was the most tragic. On August 15th, the Chopsticks Lake Embankment was breached, causing more than half of the area behind the provincial capital to be flooded. At noon on the 19th, the Wufeng Wilderness Five Li Embankment was breached, and the downstream area of the provincial capital was flooded again. The water was connected, and there was a tendency for water to enter Tongxiang Gate and Pinghu Gate. Except for a few hills, there was no dry land in the provincial capital. (Relief measures) The Emergency Relief Association office and various charitable halls send people to distribute steamed buns. In Hanyang County, the breached embankments include the Liuzhou Embankment, Xiaozhou Embankment, Liuhe Embankment, Yihe Embankment, Tiesuo Embankment, Daxing Embankment, Fuxing Embankment, Zixinshang Embankment, Changfeng Embankment, Xiexin Embankment, Tongfu Embankment, Xinglong Embankment, Mouni Embankment, Sanmin Embankment, Tongle Embankment, Fengle Embankment, Tongxing Embankment, Hexing Embankment, Duli Embankment, Xiaoyuan Embankment, Dayou Embankment, etc. During the breaching of the Dazhou Embankment, more than a hundred boaters were drowned. Most people can only travel by boat. (Relief measures) Temporarily allocate 200 shi of relief rice and telegraph the Emergency Relief Association to find ways to provide relief. In Yunmeng County, the northwest is high and flat, while the southeast is low and prone to water accumulation. Nine out of ten areas rely on embankments for flood prevention. The Fuhe Embankment is critical for the entire county. Since the breaching of the embankment and the breaches at Majia Embankment and Yujiawan, over two hundred people have been drowned. Countless large and small embankments have been breached. The flooded areas include the twelve associations of Pearl Xu Xin, etc., in the first district, the twelve associations of Xing'an Xun Jia Shangzi, etc., in the second district, the fourteen associations of Peng Jia Hejian, etc., in the third district, and the four associations of Hao Shi Tu Qiao, etc., in the fourth district. In total, more than half of the county's seventy-two associations have been flooded. (Relief measures) Temporarily allocate 600 shi of relief rice and telegraph the Emergency Relief Association to find ways to provide relief.

In Xiaogan County, the scale of the disaster area is such that not only are over ninety

embankments in the east, west, and south countryside completely submerged, but even the highlands and plains in the north countryside have also been flooded. All of the gardens, Sanbu, Jingzui, Huangxiaojie River, and the Pengjiawan area near the city, covering more than a hundred li, with residents from dozens of associations, were suddenly inundated by the swift and fierce water currents. Many men, women, old, and young were drowned because they could not escape in time. Those who survived either perched on rooftops or clung to treetops, and their cries of sorrow were unbearable to hear. In recent days, torrential rains have been continuous, and mountain floods have recurred, causing the water levels in the north and south ridges to suddenly rise several feet. The previous flood has not receded, and the subsequent flood has added to the devastation. The people are living in the midst of raging floods and have no way to survive or find food. (Relief measures) Temporarily allocate 600 shi of relief rice and telegraph the Emergency Relief Association to find ways to provide relief.

In Qianjiang County, in the first district, the Dongjing River, Tianjing Du, and Hualandi Embankments were breached, and the district was also affected by the breach of the Yuekou Xiaxi Embankment, resulting in the flooding of two-thirds of the entire district. In the second district, the Tuzhou Jiangjia Guai Xiang Embankment and Daci Pavilion Dongjing River Embankment were breached, and the entire district was submerged. In the third district, the Xijing River Changbo Hualan Embankment was breached, resulting in the flooding of one-half of the entire district. In the fourth district, the Fangjiawan Xiang Embankment was breached, resulting in the flooding of two-thirds of the entire district. In total, approximately one hundred embankments out of more than one hundred and fifty in the county's four districts are currently flooded. People have lost their homes and lack food and clothing. (Relief measures) Temporarily allocate 600 shi of relief rice and telegraph the Emergency Relief Association to find ways to provide relief.

In Yingcheng County, bordering the Yun River to the east and Taihu and Fu Rivers to the south, heavy summer rains lasted for ten days, and mountain floods erupted, causing raging waves to overflow for hundreds of li. The original embankments were all breached. Furthermore, the Han River flooded, and the downstream was blocked, causing the water level to rise daily. The county seat was also flooded. Looking from the city walls, a vast expanse of water could be seen. Countless houses were washed away, and livestock were drowned. On August 5th, thunderstorms continued throughout the night, and the floodwaters returned, turning the plains outside the city into a watery realm once again. All of the water and land crops were submerged. (Relief measures) Temporarily allocate 400 shi of relief rice and telegraph the Emergency Relief Association to find ways to provide relief.

In Qianshui County, the North Yonggan Embankment and the Yonggu Tributary Embankment were successively breached, and the Yongbao Embankment was quickly destroyed. The Maoshan Embankment Kandi was also washed away by the water due to its location downstream of Jiongfeng Ji. Fields and crops were submerged, and there is no hope for harvest. The extent of the disaster area and the severity of the disaster are unprecedented. (Relief measures) Temporarily allocate 300 shi of relief rice and telegraph the Emergency Relief Association to find ways to provide relief.

In Mianyang County, about three or four li from the Xin Embankment, there were several breaches in the Zidi Embankment of the Xiongjia Kiln on the Jiang Embankment. The Jiang Embankment in Niuze was also submerged in two places. The people's houses at the breach were damaged. As for the Xiang River, the water rose several zhang overnight, causing the Wangjiakou Hong Embankment of the Dazhu Embankment to be breached, submerging fourteen embankments and washing away more than four thousand houses. On the tenth, the water reached the Dai River, breaching and submerging seven embankments, with five breaches and washing away more than five thousand houses. In addition, the hundred-plus embankments under the jurisdiction of Pai Lake also flowed directly into the lake from the breach in the Xiang River, submerging everything completely. The Jiang Embankment in the Zhujiafeng area, more than twenty li above the Xin Embankment, and the Hujia Zhou area, more than thirty li below, were also breached in many places. The entire city of Xin Embankment became a watery realm. Furthermore, due to the breaches in the embankments of neighboring counties, eighty-nine embankments, including Guandi Cheng, were submerged. The shallow riverbed also caused fifty-nine embankments, including Wenyan Eight Cities, to be submerged. The backflow of the river also submerged the fields and houses of twenty-seven embankments, including Zhoulao Lake, and both people and livestock were drifting everywhere. (Relief measures) Temporarily allocate 600 shi of relief rice and telegraph the Emergency Relief Association to find ways to provide relief.

In Hanchuan County, the Jiangxi Embankment was breached by water in early July, causing the collapse of the adjacent Mabu Yinjia District, Danling Hechangling Embankment, and dozens of embankments in the northwest at the same time. Furthermore, the northern countryside of the county is particularly low-lying, and all the Daxing Chenjia Yongfeng Embankments were submerged. Therefore, the severity of the disaster is rare in decades. (Relief measures) Temporarily allocate 300 shi of relief rice and telegraph the Emergency Relief Association to find ways to provide relief.

In Huanggang County, with Bo'an Mountain water inside and the overflowing Jiang River outside, areas such as Niuchezui, Qiujiazui, Qiujia Shangxia Wan, Leijia Tian, Leijia Chong, Ningjia, Jiangjia Laowuzui, Jiangjia Jiang Wan, Hong Yuanjia Dawan, Caijiadun Dawan, Luojiawan, Caijiadun Fangjia Dawan, Yuanjia Dang, Yuanjia Xiaowan, and Xueyou Wan are low-lying and have long been submerged. Other embankments have been almost entirely washed away. On July 24th, torrential rains poured down, day and night, causing mountain floods to erupt. The Baixi Gui Embankment was breached by water, fields were crushed, houses were destroyed, disaster victims filled the fields, and countless people were crushed to death. (Relief measures) Temporarily allocate 500 shi of relief rice and telegraph the Emergency Relief Association to find ways to provide relief. (To be continued)

Shao Gao

Disaster Situation and Relief After the Dike Breach 52

Yangzhou Correspondence: After the breaches of the Shaobo and Gaoyou Dikes, the disaster situation has expanded. Letters and telegrams from all sides are flying, urgently seeking post-disaster measures such as saving lives, providing disaster relief, recovering corpses, and blocking breaches. The following is a selection of important news received today: Situation of Disaster in Shaogao Town: According to a report from an investigator on the ground in Gaoshao, before the Shaobo Dike was breached, a strong northwest wind blew, followed by hail. A large barge passing in front of the Guan Post Station was about to capsize. The boaters used bamboo poles to hook onto the dam stones there. Unexpectedly, when the poles were pulled out, the stones were loosened, and the lake water rushed in and collapsed. Each breach then continued to break. The north and south ends of Shao Street were severely affected, while the middle section was lighter. Salt warehouses lost about a thousand packages of edible salt. The entire city was flooded, with seven or eight out of ten houses destroyed. Countless people died. Nearby villages and towns, such as Yangjia Village and Qiaoshu Town, had similar disaster conditions. Countless people also died. Thousands of disaster victims fled to high mounds of earth to await rescue. However, the waves and water at the breaches were dangerous, and boats could not get close, leaving them helpless. Before the breach of the Gaoyou Dike, many prisoners escaped from the collapsed prison, and temporary precautions were taken, with all four gates closed. It was only when the water arrived that they realized the situation. The area outside the North Gate and the North Market bore the brunt, with a depth of about one zhang. Gaoyou's essence was originally in the North Market, which was completely washed away. Only the salt shops and the Yuhang Flour Company remained, with solid buildings that did not collapse. The salt shop staff all lived upstairs, and the two hundred-plus workers at the Yuhang Company also went upstairs to escape the disaster. They were only rescued by boat on the twenty-eighth. The middle market had higher terrain, with the highest foundation at Ma Junqing's house, which was only submerged by a foot or so and did not injure anyone. Those going to survey the disaster entered the front gate and used small boats to travel. The water at the North Gate was deep, making it impossible to travel by boat. Although the east and west gates were blocked, the city walls were on the verge of collapse. The two ends of the Jade Horse Head fell, with the middle section still remaining, with hundreds of refugees on top. However, the water was deep and the boat was dangerous, making it inconvenient to distribute relief. Only Wang Yunzhi risked his life to distribute dry food once. The water at the North Gate has now receded by more than half, with a depth of only three feet. However, corpses are everywhere inside and outside the city, all submerged in the water (because there are no coffins to collect them and no land to bury them, so no one is recovering corpses). The stench of decay fills the air, and the disaster victims there are still drinking this water. It is feared that an epidemic will inevitably break out in the future. News of Emergency Relief from the Emergency Relief Association: The Jiangdu Flood Emergency Relief Association learned on the evening of the twenty-eighth that the county magistrate had issued an order to allocate six thousand yuan to handle emergency relief. A special letter was sent to the county requesting that it be handed over to the association for distribution, or that it be distributed jointly. On the evening of the twenty-eighth, the association's chairman, Wang Jingting, dispatched vessels to rescue refugees coming to Yangzhou, totaling more than three hundred people. Except for those who were distributed to relatives and friends, thirty-seven people were admitted to the Changsheng Temple shelter. At the same time, merchants dispatched dozens of small boats to various ports to search for and rescue disaster victims and recover corpses. On the morning of the twenty-ninth, Chairman Wang also brought dozens of loads of relief grain and traveled to Gaoyou by ship to provide relief to disaster victims. In the afternoon, Vice Chairman Dai Tianqiu led four ships, carrying four hundred yuan, to the seventh and eighth districts to distribute emergency relief. All of the 1,771 yuan in national salvation funds allocated by the association for emergency relief was sent to the association by the county party department on the morning of the twenty-ninth. It is heard that, after expenses, one thousand yuan is being kept in custody by the Shengyuan Money Shop. At noon, the chairman and vice chairman of the Emergency Relief Association also telegraphed the Shanghai Chinese and Foreign Famine Relief Association, the Jiangsu Flood Relief Association, and other organizations to beg for relief. On the same day, the county government ordered the Grain Storage Association to provide three thousand yuan of accumulated grain funds for the Emergency Relief Association to use. As of the time the reporter submitted this manuscript, another one thousand several hundred refugees from Shaobo and Gaoyou had arrived, including several hundred who remained in shelters at Changsheng Temple and Zhizhu Temple. It is heard that there are still many refugees, and it is planned to send boats to transport them on the morning of the thirtieth.

Report on Relief and Disaster Survey by the Red Cross Society: Personnel from the relief team sent by the Red Cross Society to survey the disaster and provide relief, as well as personnel from the Huaiyang Charity Relief Association, returned to Yangzhou and reported that the ship could not proceed beyond Liuzha Gate. Ten-plus private boats were chartered and dragged through Kongjiawan straight down. The water at Majia Bridge was four or five feet deep. In addition, Gaofeng Bridge, Jijia Town, and Qiao Rescue Mound (with over two thousand disaster victims), Zengjiadu, Qiaoshu Town, and the Zhenwu Temple in the four countryside, Dinggou, Gaoqiao, Huanglizhuang, and Dingjiahuo (six thousand-plus households of disaster victims from Huanghualing), and Heifeng Xu with four thousand five hundred households, all suffered heavy disasters. Fields and houses were submerged, and a vast expanse of water could be seen. Corpses floated on the waves, and refugees on high ground looked forward to food like they were years old. According to the relief team's report upon returning to Yangzhou, the places affected by the water surge included Xinhekou, Diaojia Xu, Lijia Xu, Xiejiazhuang, Qianjiazhuang, Gejiazhuang, Wangjiakou, Xiajiazhuang, Daijiazhuang, Jizigou, Chenjiazhuang, Meijiazhuang, and Chenjiagou. Disaster victims were all sleeping in the open. The northwest lake area covered thousands of li, a vast expanse of water. All of the lake embankments were submerged. The breach locations included: fifteen or sixteen zhang east of Liuzha Gate, and thirteen or fourteen zhang north, all rushing towards the various counties inside the river. The Shaodi Jimaozhou South Dawang Temple was forty or fifty zhang. The Nanhétáng breach was three or four zhang, and the Nantangbian was three or four zhang. The Shi Embankment breach destroyed seven or eight out of ten rice markets. Zhuxiangkou, Guanyi, and Yan Matou destroyed the ancient Guandi Temple, Guanyi, and Public Security Bureau. Zhang Inspector's Enthusiastic Disaster Relief: Mr. Zhang Ruitang, sent by the Inspector's Office on the twenty-seventh to provide disaster relief in Shaobo and Gaoyou, has successively transported over a thousand refugees back, handing them over to Deputy Adjutant Song Bangrong, who dispatched personnel to care for them. A portion of them reside in Changsheng Temple, and food and drink are provided by the Deputy Adjutant's Office. On the morning of the twenty-ninth, Councilor Zhang Daorong and Deputy Adjutant Hu Daquan led a team of twenty-plus people, carrying food and eighteen private boats, to Xian Shao Gaoyou and other places to provide as much rescue as possible. In addition, Zhang Zhijiang and Zhang Shusheng have telegraphed Shanghai to beg for relief.

Important News on Relief Efforts in Gao Shao 53

Zhenjiang Correspondence: The breaches of the canal dikes in northern Jiangsu Province, the people who suffered, and the relief situation have been detailed in this newspaper. The following is a breakdown of the news received yesterday:

Cheng Jingsheng goes to Northern Jiangsu to Inspect the Work of the National Government Disaster Relief Committee: Mr. Cheng Jingsheng, a cadre of the working group of the National Government Disaster Relief Committee, arrived in Zhen yesterday by night train with Yuan Xiaogu and other ten-plus people. They carried approximately thirty thousand yuan in cash and purchased dry food and medicine. They departed for Yangzhou, Shaobo, Xinghua, and Gaoyou that evening. Xu Jiatang, Shi Zhiying, Yang Dehuai, Guo Fuzeng, and others from the Provincial Government accompanied them. Zhu Qinglan also telegraphed, approving his arrival in Northern Jiangsu today for inspection. Ye Chucang, Chairman of the Provincial Government, Hu Pu'an, Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, and Sun Hongzhe, Director of the Department of Construction, also plan to travel to the disaster areas of Gaoyou and Shaobo together.

Actual Situation after the Disaster in Shaobo: Since the Shaobo area experienced continuous strong winds and rain on the night of the twenty-fifth of this month, and the sudden dike breach occurred between 3:00 and 5:00 the next morning, the water spread. Lu Haishan, an inspector sent by the Department of Civil Affairs, brought dry food and rushed to investigate, and coordinated with County Magistrate Chen of Jiangdu to handle relief. Inspector Lu has now returned to the province to report, stating briefly that the water level has gradually receded in recent days, dropping more than four feet. Most of the disaster victims still wish to stay in their original locations and reorganize everything. The city of Jiangdu has set up five shelters, three of which are specifically for women and children. The disaster situation is more severe in Zhenwu Temple and Yangzhuang. Small boats have been hired to rescue people in batches, preparing to transport them to various locations in Yangzhou and Zhenjiang for resettlement. The main dam of Zhaoguan Dam has not collapsed, but the breach north of the dam is about one zhang long. The people in that area are urgently hoping that the breach will be blocked so that traffic can be restored as soon as possible, and hope that all sectors of society will provide sufficient food relief.

Li Mingyang telegraphs to report the disaster situation: Li Mingyang, Director of the Security Department, and Zhang Bin, an engineer from the Water Conservancy Bureau, went north together to investigate and sent a telegram stating briefly that north of Jieshou, except for the disaster victims scattered on the west bank, the situation on the east bank is very good. Passing through Shaobo Zhaoguan Dam, due to the large water flow, they could not land. The Huai River water is receding rapidly. The dangerous situation is not as severe as rumored. Postal and telegraph communications are not available. At 11:00 a.m., they arrived in Gaoyou and inspected on foot with local officials and gentry. Qigongdian and Longwang Temple were both washed away. Residents' houses outside the North Gate were flooded by several feet. He prays for the purchase of rice for relief.

Many breaches in the canal dike under repair: After the problems occurred in the Jiangbei Canal Dike, the Water Conservancy Bureau of the Department of Construction and its four affiliated offices have been extremely busy organizing emergency repairs, requisitioning labor, and transporting materials. The Jiangdu section was loaned a small boat from the Charity Relief Association by Director Shao to transport materials to the Shaobo area for repairs. Li Zhongqiang, the head of the Gaobao section's Public Works Office, only returned to Gaoyou yesterday to prepare for emergency repairs. It is heard that Sun Yiyi and other engineers from the Water Conservancy Bureau have recently telegraphed from Jieshou, stating that there are three breaches in the Gaoyou Dangjun Tower to Miaoxiangkou area, and more than ten problems in Yongsi Bao three flood control areas, which have been quickly repaired. They request the prompt sending of funds for relief. The Water Conservancy Bureau has continued to send multiple engineers, carrying ten thousand yuan in engineering funds, sacks, and many tools on the Fengyi boat to rush to the rescue, and has purchased two thousand branches of double-tung wood, loaded them on ships to await transport, and ordered Jiangdu County to seal up all firewood to prepare for construction use.

Minutes of the Temporary Charity Relief Conference for the Flood Disaster: The Temporary Charity Relief Conference for the Flood Disaster in Jiangbei held its first meeting of the Standing Council yesterday (30th) at 11:00 a.m., with Leng Yuqiu, Lu Xiaobo, Zhou Zigeng, Hu Jianchun, Yu Xiaochuan, and Yang Guangyu in attendance. The meeting was chaired by Leng Yuqiu. Matters for discussion: (1) The Dongtai representative recommended that Yu Ziting set sail with the ship for relief efforts. Resolution: Handed over to the relief department. (2) The association's telegram for soliciting relief was requested to be revised and approved. Resolution: Revised and approved. (3) Cheng Jingsheng, director of the Jiangsu Flood Charity Relief Association, sent a letter requesting the establishment of a resident office in the province. Resolution: (1) First, Mr. Cheng Jingsheng will be added as the vice chairman of this association. (2) The Jiangsu Flood Charity Relief Association's resident office in the province will be established immediately. All relief matters will be handled jointly by this association and that association. The office staff will also be jointly hired. (3) Funds will be signed by the chairman and vice chairman, but payment can be made with the consent of two people. (4) When requisitioning ships and relief personnel, use the flags and armbands of both associations, but the badges of this association's staff will be the badges of the Jiangsu Flood Charity Relief Association. (4) The General Affairs Department submitted a notice of item collection and purchase and a report form for approval. Resolution: Approved.

Jiangsu Charity Relief Association's telegram to Zhu Qinglan: General Zhu Jiangjun of Shanghai Yipinxiang and relayed to Chairman Xu Huangong Jian. Thank you for your telegram and for personally visiting the disaster area. In Shaoguan Town, the water has receded, and the corpses are exposed. The disaster victims are gathering. The water in the post has receded slightly, and the corpses piled up are shocking. It is unbearable to see. The disaster victims are sleeping in the open on city walls and temple roofs. The water flow is blocking the boats, making it difficult to provide relief. In addition to the two thousand-plus people already sheltered in Yangzhou and Zhenjiang, many disaster victims are still holding onto their homeland and refusing to board boats. Straw mats are not available in time, and Inspector Zhang has been telegraphed to borrow military tents for local shelters. The cash carried is exhausted. Please send a continuation as soon as possible, Cheng Jingsheng is trapped.

The Yellow River Water Level in Shandong Province is Alarming Again 54

The Luokou water level rises by six inches, Liugong is extremely dangerous

Jinan Correspondence: The water level of the Yellow River in Shandong Province, in the upper, middle, and lower reaches, has been declining for a week. However, today (the twenty-eighth), according to the water report from Shaanzhou, the water level has increased by six inches compared to a week ago, causing the water level in the upper reaches of Shandong Province to not decrease slightly, and the middle and lower reaches have also increased slightly as a result. According to today's Luokou water report, the Yellow River water level rose by six inches, with the water level 8 zhang 8 chi 6 cun above sea level. Furthermore, according to a telegram from Dongzhuang today, Director Zhang Lianjia of the River Affairs Bureau is still supervising construction in Juan territory. The seven weirs of the ten dams in Dongzhuang have been reinforced by two layers. The director will return to Jinan after the repairs are stable. The Heze Zinian has been measured, with a total length of four thousand two hundred zhang, and construction will begin within days. Furthermore, an urgent telegram from the Liuyuan section stated, "Director Zhang of the Jinan River Affairs Bureau, Section Chief Chen of the Shangshilibu Upstream Section, Qian, the dangerous situation of the Liugong has been repeatedly reported in telegrams. Now it is found that the large flow is currently impacting Dams 15, 16, and 17, with Dam 17 being the most affected. The water in front of the dam is more than three zhang deep. After the flow has impacted and scoured the dam, it is extremely dangerous. The section chief, together with the Nian Construction Bureau, has supervised soldiers and laborers to carry out emergency protection for five days and nights, raising two new sections of the embankment. Due to the tight flow and the lack of soil materials, repeated collapses have occurred. Fortunately, the soldiers and laborers have worked hard and bravely, and the situation has gradually stabilized, with the water level rising by four or five feet or more. The water in front of Dam 16 is one zhang seven or eight feet deep, and a new section of the dam has been raised, with the water level three feet higher. The dam sweep of the two dams was washed away by the flow early on. The Nian Construction Bureau has been constantly reporting this in telegrams. Recently, it has been observed that the base of the two dams is being impacted and scoured by the flow behind them, and the collapse is very rapid. The weirs should also be quickly installed to resist it. However, there is a lack of materials, which is very restrictive. In addition to urging the Nian Construction Bureau to quickly prepare, this telegram is being sent for your consideration and approval. Sincerely, Xu Desheng kowtows."

Urgent Relief Needed for the Jiujiang Flood 55

Jiujiang News: The severity of this year's Jiujiang flood is unprecedented in decades. Jiujiang, located on the Yangtze River and backed by Mount Lu, experienced continuous rain in July, causing the river to rise sharply and mountain floods to erupt. The low-lying areas in Jiujiang city, including areas such as Longkai River outside Zhonglong and Xingzhou on the riverside, began to flood on July 12th. At that time, the customs water level was only 40 feet. By the 18th, the mountain floods had further increased, and the Longkai River was blocked by the Yangtze River, unable to flow out, causing it to overflow its banks. Teahouses, restaurants, brothels, opium dens, inns, villas, and theaters of all kinds, clustered along the first, second, and third roads, were all flooded. On that day, the customs water level was 41.6 feet, on the 19th it was 41.8 feet, and on the 20th it was 42 feet. At that time, the streets and alleys along Gan Tang Lake were more than a foot deep in water. After that, the water level gradually increased. By July 29th, the entire prosperous commercial area of the city, namely the western section of Da Zhong Road, was completely submerged. All other places near the riverbanks and lakesides were filled with water. Shopkeepers opened their doors every day to watch the water, residents with multi-story houses moved to higher floors, and those without such houses relocated. The water has not receded even slightly to this day.

The entire Jiujiang county is divided into nine districts. The city is the first district, and the eighth and ninth districts are north of the Yangtze River. All the dikes and embankments have been breached in more than 30 places since July 27th, turning the area into a vast expanse of water. Even the highest points are five feet deep. Half of Jiujiang's essence is gone. The seventh district in Jiangnan suffered the most, being completely submerged with only rooftops visible. Most of the fourth and sixth districts have disappeared. The second and fifth districts are mostly mountainous and, although not directly affected by the river, have accumulated water reaching several inches in the lowest areas. In total, over 120 breaches in dikes and embankments have occurred throughout the county, affecting a disaster area of 3,710 square li. More than 154,000 people have been affected, and approximately 244,200 mu of farmland have been flooded, resulting in losses of approximately 7,327,000 yuan. More than 15,820 houses have been destroyed, resulting in losses of approximately 4,746,000 yuan. More than 1,810 people have drowned, and livestock losses are estimated at 344,000 yuan. The total losses are around 12,420,000 yuan, a disaster unprecedented in its magnitude. The commercial losses in the city are not included in this figure. The river and mountain floods are still rising today, and the scale of the future catastrophe is unknown.

In terms of relief efforts, after the most important dike in the ninth district north of the Yangtze River, named Pan Xing Dike, collapsed on August 1st, the Flood Relief Committee was established on the 2nd. Work was assigned, staff introduced, and documents processed on the 3rd, keeping everyone busy. On the 7th, the standing committee members Yuan Dinghua, Jiang Junyang, Wang Shirong, and Ye Chongru went to the provincial government to request relief funds and were approved for 3,000 yuan, which has not yet been received. At the beginning of August, there were few disaster victims coming to Xun city. Those who came either stayed with relatives and friends or rented temporary housing. These were the relatively wealthy. Later, more and more people came, with nowhere to be accommodated, scattering in empty spaces, creating a very tragic situation. Only after mid-month did they begin to provide porridge, but there was not enough to go around, so the well-fed were still full, and the hungry were still hungry. Based on the current economic situation, if no more relief funds arrive, they can maintain it until mid-September at most. Shelters have never been established, and disaster victims are sleeping outdoors and eating the wind, resulting in many deaths.

Oxen are one of the farmers' assets. When the flood came, farmland and houses could not be moved, but oxen could be led to escape. At the beginning of August, farmers bringing oxen to the city were unable to feed them and had to sell them cheaply to religious groups for slaughter with tears in their eyes. Oxen worth 70 or 80 yuan each could only be exchanged for a little over 10 yuan. Charitable people who only eat beef after slaughtering oxen showed great compassion and raised a fund of 2,000 yuan to establish a temporary oxen pawnshop. Each oxen was pawned for up to 10 yuan, and the shop hired people to graze them, allowing the farmers to redeem them at the original price in the future. This news spread, and people flocked to pawn their oxen. The pawn price was reduced from 10 to 5 yuan per oxen, and the capital was exhausted in a few days. Those who came later were still forced to enter the butcher's doors. (August 29th)

He and Chen Go to Nanchang to Meet Chiang 56

Nanchang Correspondence: He Yingqin, Commander-in-Chief of the Forward Headquarters and Commander of the Left Wing, and Chen Mingshu, Commander of the Right Wing, have been directing their troops to suppress bandits since their departure two months ago. All important bandit lairs have been successively recovered. After General Chiang returned to Jiangxi from the capital yesterday, he specially summoned He and Chen to the province to inquire about the recent battles and bandit situation, and to give them instructions in person. He and Chen, upon receiving the order, arrived in Nanchang on the 26th and visited Chiang at the headquarters one after another. He reported on the distribution of the Red bandits, their tendency to flee and cause disturbances, and the progress of the government's suppression efforts in Guangchang, Ningdu, Shicheng, Lean, and Yudu in southeastern Jiangxi and the border areas of Jiangxi and Fujian. Chen reported on the operations and progress of the suppression efforts in Ji'an, Yongfeng, Taihe, and Xingguo in southwestern Jiangxi. Chiang expressed his great satisfaction, and in addition to giving instructions in person, he also discussed future combat plans, joint advances, and methods of eradication. He and Chen stayed in the province briefly and then returned to the front separately.

It is said that General Chiang has newly formulated a bandit suppression plan. Wherever the troops go, they will completely eradicate all scattered bandits in that area, complete the household registration survey, organize a sound militia, and transform all bad elements into good citizens, without any bandits hiding among them. Only then will they advance further. (August 28th)

Liu Guitang's Troops Arrive in Juancheng 57

Gu Liangmin Goes to Intercept Them

Jinan Correspondence: Liu Guitang, the notorious, led his remaining troops of more than 500 men to Guancheng and Fanxian in western Shandong on the 26th, and then crossed the river from Pu county and fled towards Caozhou. Today (28th), the provincial government received another telegram from Liang Zaiqi, the magistrate of Juancheng county (a new county established by splitting Pu county on the south bank of the Yellow River), reporting that Liu Guitang had led his remaining troops to the vicinity west of the county seat. They refused to let him enter the city, and he immediately went south, requesting that the troops not pursue too hastily to avoid him entering the city. The current militia and public security bureau did not engage with Liu's troops.

Another report states that Liu Guitang's remaining troops broke into Yuhuangmiao and Xutang in Yuncheng on the morning of the 27th. They were fiercely surrounded and attacked by the Juancheng militia, and the bandit forces were unable to resist and fled towards Shuibu Liangshan. Gu Liangmin, commander of the 22nd Division, arrived at the junction of Yuncheng and Juye on the morning of the 27th to intercept the fleeing bandit troops. Rong Guangxing, commander of the 87th Brigade stationed in Liaocheng, also telegraphed Sun Tongxuan, the commander-in-chief of the Second Army Corps, today (28th), reporting that 200 to 300 of Liu's remaining troops suddenly broke into the Shawo area, more than 30 li north of Tangyi city. He has ordered Li's regiment of the 87th Brigade and the Tangyi militia to attack them. Li Xuande, the commander of the cavalry brigade, arrived in Pu county, and Chen Dexin, the commander of the 86th Brigade, arrived in Guancheng to direct the troops to suppress the bandits separately. According to Sun Tongxuan, the commander-in-chief of the Second Army Corps, Liu's remaining troops are no more than 700 men, harassing Yuncheng, Juye, Chaocheng, Guancheng, and Caozhou. Gu Liangmin, commander of the 22nd Division, Chen Dexin, commander of the 86th Brigade, Rong Guangxing, commander of the 87th Brigade, and Li Xuande, commander of the cavalry brigade, are currently supervising their respective units and the militias of various counties to actively suppress and attack the bandits. They should be completely eradicated within ten days. It is said that Han Fuqu has also telegraphed Sun Tongxuan and Li Shuchun, ordering them to strictly block and attack Liu's bandits. However, Gu Liangmin also sent a telegram to Sun Tongxuan and others yesterday, reporting on the recent situation of bandit suppression in western Shandong. The telegram reads: "To Commander Sun Tongxuan and Commander Cao Fulin of Qing, greetings. Your telegrams of Chen Wu are noted. Zi Mi, I led my troops to the junction of Ju and Yun on the day of Gan to intercept the enemy and ordered them to defend. According to reports from the Yuncheng militia, Liu Hei Qi led his troops of approximately 500 men into Yuhuangmiao and Xutang in Yuncheng. I immediately led my troops to attack, killing over 20 bandits and wounding dozens. The bandit forces were unable to resist and fled towards Shuibu Liangshan, and so on. I am reporting this. Your respectful servant, Gu Liangmin, bows." (August 28th)

Changsha's Finance Returns to Normal 59

Reason: Withdrawal of Guangdong-Guangxi Armies

Hengbao Areas Also Lifted Martial Law

Changsha Correspondence: The rumors of the Guangdong-Guangxi armies' plot to invade Hunan have subsided, and the border defenses of Hunan have transitioned from tension to peace. Martial law in Hengzhou and Baoqing has been lifted. Looking back to half a month ago, due to the increasing rumors of Guangdong and Guangxi plotting to invade Hunan, various banks and money houses transported cash to Shanghai and Hankou, causing a financial panic due to the lack of cash in the market. Interest rates in the market increased, with the interest on every 1,000 yuan rising to 20 yuan every half month, and Shanghai notes falling to 97 (only worth 97 yuan per 100 yuan), an unprecedented anomaly in the Changsha market. Since the withdrawal of the Guangdong-Guangxi armies, the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications have successively transported hundreds of thousands of yuan of cash from Hankou, and the interest rate has fallen from 20 yuan to 7 yuan, and Shanghai notes have risen from 97 to 98.5. The financial situation in the market has returned to normal.

Yesterday, He Jian received a report from Yongzhou stating that Zhang Gui's army had all returned to Pingle, Gongcheng, and Guilin, and there were no signs of plotting to invade Hunan for the time being. He Jian reported this to General Chiang, He Yingqin, He Chengjun, and others. The telegram reads as follows: "(1) I have just received a telegram from Yongzhou reporting that Wu Qiwai's division of Zhang Fakui's troops has moved from Longhuguan and Xilingzhai to Ping (Le) Gong (Cheng). Another regiment has moved to Guilin. Wei Yunzhong and Huang Heling's two divisions have moved from Pinggong to the Wuxun area. Li Pinxian's division has one regiment stationed in Guilin, and the rest have moved to Pingle. Han Caifeng's division has moved to Liuzhou Changping. Tan Lianfang's battalion is stationed on the west bank of the Huangsha River. There are no troops stationed in Meixikou and Guanyang. (2) The Guangxi army is composed of 20,000 newly recruited soldiers who have not completed two months of training. Half of them will be kept for future recruitment, and the rest will be transported to Guangdong. It is said that they are tricking Chen Jitang into providing them with weapons, but he has only promised to allocate 1,000 rifles, which have not yet arrived. Recently, many new recruits have deserted from various units. (3) Li Zongren stayed in Guangdong, and Zhang Fakui stayed in Hong Kong, and both have not returned to Guangxi. Bai Chongxi has also recently gone from Guangxi to Wu, and there are currently no signs of plotting to invade Guangdong or Hunan." I especially report. Your respectful servant, He Jian, bows.

When the rumors of the Guangdong-Guangxi armies' plot to invade Hunan reached Hunan, He Jian had transferred all of Tao Guang's 31st Division to Hengzhou for defense. Now that the situation has eased, He Jian has ordered Tao's division to transfer a brigade to Gongyou to cooperate with Jiangxi Lianhua in suppressing Li Mingrui's bandits. (August 27th)

Germany

Female Aviator Ms. Yederu Arrives in Shenyang 60

Comparable to Amy Johnson

Shenyang Correspondence: German female aviator Ms. Yederu, after departing from Germany via Siberia, arrived in Harbin on the 25th and left Harbin at 3 PM on the 26th for Shenyang. The Aviation Command, after receiving a report from Zen Chen Foreign Company stating that Ms. Ye would arrive today, immediately prepared to receive her. Later, due to cloudy and rainy weather, they were concerned that she would not be able to arrive as scheduled. It wasn't until 5 PM that the German Consulate received a confirmed telegram stating that Ye had left Harbin and, barring any obstacles en route, would arrive in Shenyang at around 6 PM. The Consulate immediately notified overseas Chinese in Shenyang and our government officials. The Aviation Command dispatched staff member Xu Shangzhang, translator Li Cunxin, and technician Jiang Changying to be responsible for the reception. At around 5 PM, Yu Lianzuo, secretary of the European and American Section of the Diplomatic Commissioner's Office, the German Consul-General stationed in Liaoning, various overseas merchants, and reporters from Chinese and foreign newspapers rushed to the venue in the rain to welcome her. At 5:50 PM, a black dot appeared in the northwestern sky. German overseas merchants took off their hats and cheered wildly, and the atmosphere was immediately enthusiastic. Soon after, the sound of the engine was heard. In about five minutes, the plane landed safely on the field. The German Consul and overseas merchants rushed forward to push the plane and presented flowers. The plane was a yellow, single-winged Junkers A50 model with 88 and 8/10 horsepower. Ms. Ye was wearing a yellow leather flying suit, goggles, and yellow leather shoes. Her complexion was tan, indicating that she had endured wind and frost. After disembarking, she shook hands and exchanged pleasantries with the crowd. The Chinese side presented a cup of champagne as a tribute and expressed their condolences. Ms. Ye smiled and thanked them. She then went to the Aviation Command's reception room to rest and have refreshments. She was then hosted by the German Consul and lodged in the German Club on Er Jing Liu Wei Road. It is said that Ms. Ye traveled from Germany to Shenyang in seven days, covering a distance of 34,000 kilometers. She plans to leave Shenyang on the 27th and go to Tokyo. After staying for one or two days, she will return to our country, pass through Shanghai and Qingdao, and then go to India and return home. Ms. Ye is following in the footsteps of Amy Johnson by flying alone to Shenyang, and her achievements are comparable, which is highly valued by all parties. It can also stimulate people's interest in aviation. (August 26th)

Memorial Service for Overseas Chinese in Korea 61

77th Day Since Overseas Chinese Were Killed

Survivors Shed Tears Together

Andong Correspondence: Korean thugs recently massacred overseas Chinese, resulting in an unprecedented bloody tragedy. The 77th day since the tragic deaths of the overseas Chinese has already passed, but this major tragedy seems to have faded into oblivion. Not only has it failed to inspire the patriotism of the Chinese people, but the hundreds of overseas Chinese who died tragically will have difficulty finding peace under the Nine Springs. Recently, the Chinese Chamber of Commerce in the capital, in order to commemorate the tragically deceased overseas Chinese and to arouse the patriotism of the Chinese people, designated the 22nd of this month as the 77th day since the tragic deaths of the overseas Chinese, and held a large-scale memorial service to express grief. After the Chamber of Commerce proposed this idea, the overseas Chinese in Korea unanimously sympathized with it. Therefore, on the 22nd, the Chinese Chambers of Commerce in Incheon, Pyongyang, Wonsan, Sinuiju, and other places all held memorial services for the deceased overseas Chinese. All the surviving overseas Chinese in Korea shed tears together. According to a guest returning from Sinuiju, the chairman of the Chinese Chamber of Commerce in Sinuiju, Mr. Han, received a special letter from the Chinese Chamber of Commerce in the capital five days ago notifying him to hold a memorial service. He immediately began preparations. On the morning of the 22nd, the memorial service was held in the auditorium of the Chinese Commercial Primary School. In the center of the auditorium were portraits and wills of General Sun Yat-sen and party and national flags. Below, on a table, were arranged the spiritual tablets of the deceased overseas Chinese, about two feet high, inscribed with "Spiritual Tablets of the Deceased Overseas Chinese in Korea". In front of the offering table were arranged incense burners, candlesticks, clear wine, and vegetarian dishes. On both sides were hung wreaths and elegiac couplets. At this time, 600 to 700 overseas Chinese came uninvited. At about 10:00 AM, the meeting began according to the scheduled ceremony. Chairman Han gave the opening address, and Consul Zhu took the stage to give a speech that was tragic and moving. Other guests also gave speeches separately, their words were extremely sad. It wasn't until about 1:00 PM that the meeting was adjourned. Although the Japanese police station did not object to the meeting on the surface, they paid special attention to it, so they dispatched several plainclothes patrol officers to the venue to monitor it. (August 25th)

Nanhui

Violent Winds and Rain Cause Disaster: On the evening of August 25th, violent winds and rain ravaged Nanhui County. The cotton and rice fields in the county were blown by the wind and rain, and the cotton bolls and yellow flowers were all knocked down, and the rice grains were damaged and looked desolate. Along the coast of the county, the embankments in the group districts were broken in more than 20 places by the tide. The Huijiao Dike in the fifth district was also broken in more than 20 zhang. A Wanghai tower guarding against pirates was also blown down. The thatched houses of poor farmers along the coast were all destroyed. East of Wangtang, the water is about four feet deep, and many farmers have nowhere to live. It is now known that the district chiefs, Zhang Yiyi and others, have reported to the county government one after another, requesting that measures be taken for relief. A Record of the Trial of an Evil Prank Case: The case of a wife's adultery and a husband's evil prank that occurred on North Gate Street in this city has been reported in this newspaper. It is now known that Mei Qiushi could not be treated by the Public First Hospital and was transferred to the Shanghai Labor Hospital, but the treatment was ineffective, and she has died. Yesterday, the county government opened a trial of this case. Judge Lu presided over the trial. First, Mei Kui-ru, the husband of Mei Qiushi, was questioned. (Question) Why did you insert an iron bar into your wife Qiushi's lower body? (Answer) There was no such thing. That night, I wanted to sleep with her, but she refused, so we had a verbal argument and a scuffle. (Question) Where did the blood all over the bed come from? (Answer) It was really because she was having her period. (Question) Your wife is now dead, do you know that? (Answer) I know that. Her coffin has already been brought back from Shanghai. I am really wronged in this matter. I beg for a clear investigation. Then, Zhang Qiushi, the elder sister of Mei, and Zhao Shenshi, the mother of Mei, were questioned. It was said that this case was reported by you and others. Now, the father is requesting that the case be withdrawn. How much money did you get from Mei Kui-ru? They replied that they did not get any money. They really pitied him for being so miserable, so they voluntarily withdrew the case. At this point, Mei Kui-ru was ordered to be detained for further investigation and determination.

Songjiang 63

Continued Report on the Story of a Patrol Officer Demanding Pay and Insulting the District Chief: Yesterday (29th), the story of a patrol officer from the Fourth Precinct of this city demanding pay and insulting the district chief was briefly reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now known that the police expenses of the Fourth Precinct of the city have always been insufficient to cover the expenses. Moreover, since August of last year, more than ten additional police officers have been added, further increasing police expenses. At that time, the salaries of the detectives of the County Public Security Bureau were also paid separately by the First District Office from the housing police donation item on a monthly basis. However, the County Bureau's own expenses were also insufficient to cover the expenses. Therefore, from the 19th year of the Republic of China, the county magistrate ordered the First District Office to allocate funds from the housing police donation item. However, the First District's housing police donation revenue was limited, and it was really unable to cope with the heavy burden. This time, two-thirds of the Fourth Precinct's police pay for July has been paid, and there is still a small amount left. They originally planned to borrow money from the bank yesterday to cope with it. Unexpectedly, the patrol officer and others, without asking the reason, cleverly induced District Chief Zhong to go to the Public Security Bureau and placed him under house arrest, subjecting him to all kinds of insults. After repeated explanations, they turned a deaf ear. At that time, the Bureau Chief was at the side but did not stop them, which was very strange. Later, the First District Office staff reported to the County Magistrate, who telegraphed the Bureau Chief to stop them, and he was released back to the office. It is now heard that the County Government will severely punish the Bureau Chief and the Patrol Officer for condoning their subordinates, insulting the District Chief, and having no ability to control them. District Chief Zhong, who has suffered this strange insult, is said to be preparing a written report of the incident to the Chamber of Commerce and the shopkeepers who pay the donation, seeking public opinion.

County Government Grain Storage Conference: The Civil Affairs Department specially dispatched Commissioner Wu Xie to Songjiang in order to prepare for the grain storage in various counties to replenish their stocks. He once convened a meeting with the food management committee and convened leaders of the County Party Department, various agencies, and district chiefs at the County Government a few days ago. County Magistrate Shen presided over the meeting. Commissioner Wu reported on the main intentions of the Civil Affairs Department, which were to not allow the accumulation of money for grain storage and to expand and recover the methods of transfer and misappropriation. Matters discussed: (1) It was resolved to spend all the accumulated money to purchase white rice for storage within the time limit stipulated by the Civil Affairs Department. (2) It was resolved that A. Starting from the busy season of the 21st year of the Republic of China, two cents per mu will be levied. B. Various stores will donate one-thousandth of their capital amount based on the business tax survey. The Chamber of Commerce will notify them. C. Following the Jinshan method, one sheng of rice per mu will be assigned from the ripe fields, and the landlords will collect it from the farmers to offset the rent. D. Items B and C will be limited to one year for the time being. Detailed measures will be submitted to the County Government Conference for review. (3) The County Government will follow orders to investigate and recover the grain storage funds that have been withdrawn for military expenses and other expenses over the years.

Chamber of Commerce Raises Disaster Relief Funds: The County Chamber of Commerce held a regular meeting yesterday to discuss matters. Regarding the floods in various places, the Chamber of Commerce decided to raise funds for relief from various businesses and shops. At the same time, they will send representatives to Shanghai to contact the Flood Relief Association to distribute the funds on their behalf. A corrected version of the Chamber of Commerce's budget for the 20th year of the Republic of China was passed and submitted to the Supervisory Committee for review and implementation.

Zhenjiang 68

County Government Distributes Urgent Relief in Zhenjiang County. The county government of Zhenjiang has received successive reports from districts 157 that dikes have broken, and livestock and houses have been swept away by the waves. Disaster victims are either clinging to tree branches or on dikes, urgently needing relief. Jiangbei Disaster Area: Boats Rescue Disaster Victims. The scale of this Jiangbei flood is truly unprecedented. Although the severity of the disaster in various places has been repeatedly reported in newspapers, inquiries from various sources have led to diverse and unclear information. There is still no news from Xinghua, Dongtai, Yancheng, and Funing. Yesterday, the provincial government dispatched six boats, towing civilian boats loaded with dry food and relief funds, to various disaster-stricken counties for relief. The Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce recently received an urgent telegram from Qingjiangpu, requesting boats for rescue. Small steamers between Yangzhou and Zhenjiang are all being used for disaster relief. However, information is blocked from counties along the Xiangxia River, and transportation is cut off. If maritime charitable organizations could provide boats for rescue in the disaster area, it would be truly meritorious.

Gaoyou 69

The Right to Manage the Chen Gong Ancestral Hall Property Has Been Determined. The ancestral property of Chen Guorui's ancestral hall, a famous general of the Qing Dynasty, is located in Minjiaqiao Town, Huxi, Gaoyou County. Previously, it was managed by local gentry appointed by the county government. The rent from the ancestral fields was used for the repair and maintenance of the ancestral hall and its sacrificial ceremonies, with the remaining funds allocated to the county's education expenses. However, in recent years, a descendant of Chen Gong, Chen Dazhi, suddenly disputed the ownership of the ancestral fields. The Jiangsu Provincial Government ruled that the ancestral fields belonged to the ancestral hall. Since the management rights were not determined, Chen Dazhi, based on the order that the fields belonged to the ancestral hall, requested the judicial administration office to recover the ancestral fields and hand them over to the Hubei Fellow Villagers Association for management. The various agencies of this county disagreed with the decision of the Jiangsu Provincial Government and petitioned the Ministry of Interior, requesting a determination of the management rights. Now, the county government has received an order from the provincial government forwarding a decision from the Ministry of Interior. The main points are: (To supplement the decision of the Jiangsu Provincial Government that the ancestral property of Chen Guorui's ancestral hall belongs to the ancestral hall, a board of directors should be organized according to law to manage it, supervised by the Gaoyou County Government. The profits should be used for sacrificial ceremonies and annual repairs of the ancestral hall, with the remaining funds allocated to the county's education expenses.)

Hangzhou 70

The Department of Finance Borrows Another 700,000 Yuan from Banks. The Zhejiang Department of Finance is facing empty provincial coffers and a shortage of financial resources. Despite repeated borrowing to maintain operations, it is still insufficient to cope with expenses. With the end of the month approaching, military and political expenses are long overdue, and demands for allocation are urgent. Department Director Wang Chengying has negotiated with the banking sector to borrow funds, including 500,000 yuan from the Bank of China in Hangzhou and 200,000 yuan from the Shanghai Siming Bank, using 1.2 million yuan in old outstanding public bonds as collateral, with a monthly interest rate of 1.2%. An agreement has been reached with the authorities of both banks, and the contract was signed yesterday for the actual transfer of funds.

The Verdict on the Appeal of a Murder Case. The case of Shaoxing farmers Shen Changyou and others for murder has been concluded after the initial judgment by the local branch court and subsequent appeal and trial in Hangzhou. Yesterday, Shen Changyou was sentenced to twelve years of imprisonment for the crime of jointly plotting murder, with two days of detention counting as one day of imprisonment. The trial procedures for Shen Qian, Shen Shunfeng, Zhou Chunfa, and others were suspended.

Jiaxing 71

Statistics on the Disaster Situation in Jiaxing. Jiaxing previously suffered a disaster due to continuous rain, and all the crops were submerged. Although farmers tried their best to drain the water, the results were minimal. The county government repeatedly received telegrams from district offices, village and neighborhood associations, township farmers' associations, and villagers reporting the disaster situation. They dispatched personnel to various townships for on-site investigation, which has now been completed. A total of 2,509 households have been affected in the county, with 12,658 people affected. 21,018 mu of fields have been destroyed. It is estimated that the autumn harvest will be reduced by about 50%. The county is now compiling a list to report to the province for review.

Demolition of the Qianxi Dang Fish Weir. The Xinyi Company in Shuangqiao District, Jiaxing, had built weirs in Qianjia Dang, which were strong and obstructed the flow of water. Local villagers petitioned the county government to send personnel to demolish them. County Magistrate Liang and Director of the Construction Bureau personally went to the countryside to investigate and confirmed the facts, and submitted a report to the Construction Department for approval. The Construction Department has now ordered the county to demolish them. Therefore, the county government yesterday dispatched District Chief Mei Shuren, together with Police Chief Gao, leading police officers, to quickly demolish all the weirs built by Xinyi Company in Qianjia Dang.

Ningbo 72

The Self-Defense Corps Repels a Large Band of Bandits. Chen Shizhong, the head of the Fenghua Zuoxikeng Self-Defense Corps, received a report on the 26th that Sun Libiao, a bandit leader pursued by the First Battalion of the Sheng County Security Team, would likely flee into Fenghua. He led over ten members of the corps, including Wang Qizheng, to block the Tangwu Ridge on the border of Sheng and Fenghua. Around 3:00 AM that night, over forty bandits approached from the ridge road. The corps members shouted inquiries, and the bandits immediately opened fire. The corps members returned fire for ten minutes, and the bandits fled in all directions. One bandit was killed on the spot, and a Browning pistol was found on the bandit's body. On the afternoon of the 27th, the bandit's body was taken to the city for inspection.

Hankou Disaster Victims Arrive. The Ningbo Fellow Villagers Association and the Shaoxing Fellow Villagers Association, considering the severe flooding in Hankou, previously dispatched two ships, the Xinning and the Xinghan, to Hankou to transport disaster victims back to their ancestral homes in Ningbo and Shaoxing. The Xinning ship set sail on the morning of the 26th, heading directly to Ningbo, and arrived last night at 8:00 PM, carrying over a thousand passengers. All their fares, food expenses, and wine expenses were waived. The Xinghan ship will depart today and is expected to arrive on the 31st.

Pinghu 73

Investigating the Case of Embezzlement of Corpse's Wealth. Dai Rongsheng, a resident of the outer sea of Zhapu, previously salvaged a corpse containing a large amount of banknotes and several gold rings. He reported it to the Zhapu Public Security Bureau for collection. Bureau Chief Fang Menggeng did not report it to the public and embezzled 1,300 yuan of the banknotes and silver. After County Magistrate Wu learned of this, Fang was dismissed from his post, and the current Bureau Chief Cheng Rongzhou was ordered to summon Dai Rongsheng to the county for questioning and report the matter to the province for handling.

Discovery of Military Supplies Buried by Mutinous Soldiers. During the mutiny of the soldiers of the Sixteenth Company of Xincang stationed at the sandy land behind the Damao Mountain in Changshan Village, Zhapu, two rifles, a large knife, and seventy-nine bullets were buried. Recently, they were exposed by tidal erosion. Yesterday, they were discovered by a resident, Huang Er, and handed over to the Second District Office for forwarding to the county government for inspection.

Anqing 74

Anhui Province Will Add a New County Seat. Between Chuzhou, Lai'an, and Dingyuan Counties in Anhui Province, there is Sanjie Town. The area is far from the county seats of the four counties, surrounded by mountains, and plagued by bandits. Shao Shugu, a local gentry, previously submitted a petition to the Ministry of Interior to establish a new county seat in the area, proposing the new county name to be Jiashan County. The provincial government sent an inspector, Yang Hongbin, to investigate and convened a meeting in Sanjie Town with the county magistrates of Lai'an, Chuzhou, and Dingyuan for discussion. All were in favor. The matter is now being reported back to the provincial government for review.

The New County Magistrate Changes Again. Zhang Shusen, the county magistrate of Hefei, has been transferred to another county. The newly appointed Ju Zhou Junnan has not yet arrived in Hefei. Various public organizations have telegraphed the province to urge him to take office. The reply was that Zhou could not take office due to personal matters. The provincial government decided to transfer Zhu Tingliao, the county magistrate of Langxi, to Hefei and has telegraphed him to take office.

Education News

Special Article

What is the Use of Remedial Education? 75

Jiang Wenyu (3)

(3) In terms of level, it should be divided into several grades. The lowest grade is equivalent to elementary school. As mentioned in the previous article, this is of course a special situation in China. However, even for the elementary level, a part of the teaching materials suitable for children under the age of ten should be removed, and vocational training should be added. The elementary grade is equivalent to senior elementary school, the intermediate grade is equivalent to junior high school, and the advanced grade is equivalent to senior high school. These three grades can be said to be the mainstream of remedial education. Beyond this, there is also the highest grade, which is equivalent to the first and second years of vocational school. It seems appropriate to prepare all five grades to meet the needs of all parties in society. If it is further expanded, such as night universities and academic lectures, it will be almost equivalent to part of the university curriculum.

This is the remedial education I advocate, which can exert great power and solve the difficult problems of Chinese education.

Let us try to calmly observe the actual situation in China. Does the general society feel that school education is too unsuitable for China's economic and social conditions? A middle school student costs two to three hundred yuan a year, and a university student costs four to five hundred yuan a year. How can a middle-class family afford it? If they can't afford it but insist on doing it, it's no wonder there are complaints everywhere. Not to mention those who study, who are full of complaints, even those who run schools, because public and private finances are very difficult, are also frowning and sighing. We have personally seen many talented students who could indeed be cultivated into outstanding talents, but because their families are poor and unable to support them, they cannot continue to advance after graduating from elementary school, and they cannot continue to study after graduating from middle school. Is this not a great loss to the country? At the same time, there is also a group of young people with not very high qualifications who, because of the instigation of vanity, become groups of people going to those boring universities. After four years of studying and spending thousands of dollars, they are still unemployed. Is this not a great danger to the country? Middle school education is aimed at preparing for further education, but the universities they are admitted to are like this. Year after year, many university graduates are produced, spread in society, bumping around, and no one cares about them anymore. Those who graduate from middle school and do not go to university are not willing to lower their ambitions and learn agriculture, engineering, or commerce. If they are unwilling to learn, they are also bumping around in society, and no one cares about them even more. Fortunately, vocational education has been promoted by the government and advocated by the society. However, school equipment requires money, and teachers take time to train. How can many be established at once? Even if many are established, how can they all be run well at once? (Distant water cannot quench near thirst) What should we do? Is this not the real situation in Chinese society today?

I will not avoid being verbose and will further explain separately from the perspectives of urban and rural areas. In urban areas, among the workers and apprentices in factories or shops who have graduated from elementary or junior high school and are aspiring to advance but have no opportunity, there are indeed more and more every day. This group of young people can be regarded as social producers. They are willing to study in their spare time, which does not cost their parents a penny. Unfortunately, the country and society do not have many appropriate educational institutions to meet their needs. This is so pitiful. In rural areas, elementary schools are currently as rare as morning stars, so very few people are literate. However, a group of young people around the age of twenty who are engaged in farming have leisure time to sit in teahouses and wander around idly, and sometimes they also feel the pain of being illiterate and having no knowledge. They are willing to read and open their eyes, but there are not many appropriate educational institutions now, which makes them forever fall into the dark world. This is also so pitiful.

Important News

Ministry of Education Orders Report

Trial Implementation of New Local Education Administrative System 76

The Ministry of Education ordered the reporting of the trial implementation of the new local education administrative system. In addition to ordering all trial areas directly under the Executive Yuan, it also issued a general order to the education departments of all provinces, saying: "Recently, various local education administrative agencies have been trying out new systems for the organization of local education administration, such as the central elementary school system and provincial, municipal, and county counseling conferences. Their impact on local education is not insignificant. However, the Ministry of Education urgently wants to know the details of the trial implementation of these systems, including how the measures are implemented, what the regulations are, what preparations were made before the trial, what difficulties were encountered during the trial, what achievements were made after the trial, and whether they can be universally promoted throughout the country, so as to provide a reference for improving the national local education administration. If the education department and its subordinate counties and cities are trying out this system, they should submit a detailed report separately within the shortest possible time and send it to the Ministry of Education for verification and handling."

Ministry of Education

Instructs Gansu Education Department on Normal School System 77

The Ministry of Education, according to the report submitted by the Gansu Education Department forwarding the enrollment list of students in the four-two system pre-service normal school general course of the Provincial Sixth Normal School, requested review and approval for record. The Ministry of Education instructed: "The submitted report is acknowledged. After checking the qualifications of the students listed in the school's report, there are no discrepancies. Approval is granted for record. However, the name 'pre-service normal school general course' is not appropriate. According to the regulations for normal schools, they should enroll junior high school graduates and provide them with three years of training. If it is for cultivating rapid-training teachers, they should enroll senior elementary school graduates and provide them with several years of training, which can be called a 'several-year system teacher training class.' Please instruct the school to comply with this and change the class to a 'four-year system teacher training class.'"

The Battle was Decided in Four Sets

Mr. Tawara is Talented

Machida's Skills Were Inferior

2-6

6-4

As Easy as Flipping a Hand - In the first set, Qiu and Jiang's performance plummeted, which was disappointing. (From Right to Left) Qiu Feihai (China), Jiang Daozhang (China), Tawara Sekio (Japan), Machida (Japan) (Photo by Wang Kai)

Local News

Zhu Qinglan

Discussing the Disaster Situation in Jiangbei 93

Flew Over Jiangbei for a Week Yesterday and Returned to Shanghai on the Same Day – The Disaster Situation in Shaobo, Gaoyou, and Xinghua is More Severe – Jieshou, Sishui, and Baoying Areas are Relatively Prosperous – Zhu Qinglan, a member of the National Government's Relief Committee for Water Disasters, visited Jiangbei after the dikes of the Grand Canal broke, causing many areas to be flooded. He took a plane from the Shanghai Hongqiao Airport at 8 a.m. yesterday, accompanied by Mr. Shi Dupei, the chief engineer of the Yangtze River, and engineer Zhou Xiangxian, to Nanjing and then to Jiangbei to fly over and inspect the water disaster in various counties along the Grand Canal. After departing yesterday morning, Zhu and others completed their inspection in the afternoon and returned to Shanghai on the same plane, landing at Hongqiao Airport at 2:30 p.m. yesterday. They immediately went to the residence of Song Ziwen, the chairman of the National Government's Relief Committee for Water Disasters, on Bixun Road in the French Concession, to report. They returned to their residences for rest at around 5 p.m. A reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency visited Mr. Zhu after hearing of his return to Shanghai. According to his account of the water disaster situation in Jiangbei after flying over the area yesterday, he said, "I departed at around 8 a.m. this morning with the chief engineer of the Yangtze River and others on a China National Aviation Corporation plane, first to Nanjing to refuel, and then via Longtan, Yizheng (Shi'erxu), Yangzhou, to Shaobo, Gaoyou, along the Grand Canal, to Jieshou, Sishui, Baoying, Xinghua, and other places, flying around for a week before returning. On the way, because the plane we were on was a land plane, we did not stop anywhere. However, when inspecting the disaster areas, the plane flew very low, so the inspection was very clear. The disaster situation in Shaobo, Gaoyou, and Xinghua is quite severe, but not as severe as reported in the newspapers. The rumor that Gaoshao is completely submerged is not accurate. When we inspected, we saw that Gaoyou City was still completely intact, and the houses built on high ground were still standing. Even in the low-lying areas, the roofs were still visible above the water. The city itself is in good condition, only the east, west, and north sides are more severely affected. Going north from here, from Jieshou through Sishui to Baoying County, everything is still intact. I saw that the area from Jieshou to Baoying is relatively prosperous, while in Xinghua County, the disaster situation is more severe, with fourteen breaches in the city walls."

Mr. Baker 94

Reports on the Disaster Situation in Wuhan 95

Proof of the Chinese People's Resilience

Admirable Official and Commercial Disaster Relief Efforts

Necessity of Providing Relief Goods and Funds

The National Government's Relief Committee for Water Disasters previously sent engineer Baker to Wuhan to inspect the disaster situation. He returned to Shanghai on the 29th of this month. According to his report on the situation in Wuhan, the Chinese people have always possessed strong resilience. This Wuhan water disaster further proves this. Although the water in Hankou has not yet receded, vendors have already been able to place groceries and other items in wooden buckets, wading through the water to peddle them door to door. Merchants have also prepared to repair the city walls and damaged houses. Officials and bankers are also preparing to rebuild the shanty areas destroyed by the floods into new urban areas.

Mr. Baker deeply admired the swift and cooperative disaster relief efforts of officials and merchants in the three towns of Wuhan. The Wuhan Chamber of Commerce was able to gather 140 private organizations and 30 charitable institutions to handle emergency relief matters, demonstrating considerable魄力.

Many Chinese and foreign merchants have converted their warehouses into shelters for disaster victims. Residents have also been able to rescue people drifting in the water and help them onto their buildings, providing temporary accommodation until they can be moved to various shelters. Most of the food for the disaster victims is provided by the aforementioned merchants and residents, and some is distributed by the Chamber of Commerce.

Mr. Baker believes that the Relief Committee for Water Disasters should first establish a branch in Wuhan to cooperate with local officials and merchants. Emergency relief in Wuhan has already made some progress, but local financial resources and food supplies are nearing exhaustion. It is necessary for official and charitable relief organizations to quickly transport relief goods and provide financial assistance. Organizing a sound relief organization and dispatching technical personnel to repair dikes are also urgent tasks at present.

This is no ordinary disaster and cannot be handled alone. All generous benefactors must understand this.
